# Purgatorio - Canto 18

### 1 Posto avea fine al suo ragionamento

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: The lofty teacher had brought his discourse to an end,
- **gemini1-ja**: 高貴な学者はその話を終え

- **gemma3-en**: Had placed an end to his reasoning
- **gemma3-ja**: 高い教師は彼の推論を終え、

- **gptoss-en**: Place had end to his reasoning  
- **gptoss-ja**: 彼は自分の議論に終わりを置いた

### 2 l’alto dottore, e attento guardava

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and he gazed intently
- **gemini1-ja**: 私が満足しているかどうかを注意深く私の様子を見ていた

- **gemma3-ja**: 注意深く見つめ、

### 3 ne la mia vista s’io parea contento;

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: into my face to see if I seemed content;
- **gemini1-ja**: 私の視線の中に

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: into my sight if I appeared content;
- **gemma3-ja**: 私の視線が満足しているように見えたかどうかを観察していた。

- **gemini1-en**: is drawn to everything that pleases it,
- **gemini1-ja**: すぐに気に入ったものには何でも移ろいやすく、

### 21 tosto che dal piacere in atto è desto.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: as soon as it is awakened to action by pleasure.
- **gemini1-ja**: 快楽が実際に起こるとすぐに目覚める。

### 22 Vostra apprensiva da esser verace

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: Your apprehensive faculty, in order to be true,
- **gemini1-ja**: 真実であるべきあなたの理解は
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>Vostra</td><td>apprensiva</td><td>da</td><td>esser</td><td>verace</td></tr>

<tr><th>Gender</th><td>f.</td><td>f.</td><td></td><td>m.</td><td>m.</td></tr>
<tr><th>Number</th><td>sg.</td><td>sg.</td><td></td><td>sg.</td><td>sg.</td></tr>
<tr><th>Tense</th><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>present</td><td></td></tr>
<tr><th>Mood</th><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>infinitive</td><td></td></tr>
<tr><th>English</th><td>your</td><td>apprehensive</td><td>from</td><td>being</td><td>true</td></tr>
<tr><th>Latin</th><td>vester</td><td>apprehensivus</td><td>de + ad</td><td>esse</td><td>verax</td></tr>
<tr><th>Interlingua</th><td>vostre</td><td>apprehensiva</td><td>de</td><td>esser</td><td>verace</td></tr>

<tr><th>Spanish</th><td>vuestra</td><td>aprensiva</td><td>de</td><td>siendo</td><td>veraz</td></tr>
<tr><th>Portuguese</th><td>vossa</td><td>apreensiva</td><td>de</td><td>sendo</td><td>verdadeiro</td></tr>
<tr><th>Romanian</th><td>vostru</td><td>temătoare</td><td>de</td><td>fiind</td><td>adevărat</td></tr>
<tr><th>Esperanto</th><td>via</td><td>timema</td><td>de</td><td>estante</td><td>vera</td></tr>
<tr><th>Derived</th><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td></tr>
<tr><th>Etymology</th><td>voster</td><td>apprehendere</td><td>de + ad</td><td>esse</td><td>verax</td></tr>
</table>

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: Your apprehension to be truthful
- **gemma3-ja**: あなたの理解は真実であろうとすることから
<table>

### 27 che per piacer di novo in voi si lega.

### 45 se dritta o torta va, non è suo merto».

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: it is no merit of hers whether she goes straight or crooked.”
- **gemini1-ja**: それが正しいか間違っているかは、魂の功績ではありません。」

### 54 come per verdi fronde in pianta vita.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: just as the life in a plant is revealed through its green leaves.
- **gemini1-ja**: 植物の緑の葉のように。

### 116 che restar non potem; però perdona,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: that we cannot stop; therefore forgive us
- **gemini1-ja**: 止まることはできません。ですから、許してください。

### 128 tant’ era già di là da noi trascorso;

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: so far beyond us had he already passed;

### 129 ma questo intesi, e ritener mi piacque.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: but this I heard, and it pleased me to remember it.
- **gemini1-ja**: しかし、私はこれを聞いて、覚えておくことにしました。

### 145 e ’l pensamento in sogno trasmutai.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and transformed my thoughts into a dream.
- **gemini1-ja**: そして、考えは夢へと変わった。
